3331 //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
3332 
3333 void MacroAssembler::clear_jweak_tag(Register possibly_jweak) {
3334   const int32_t inverted_jweak_mask = ~static_cast<int32_t>(JNIHandles::weak_tag_mask);
3335   STATIC_ASSERT(inverted_jweak_mask == -2); // otherwise check this code
3336   // The inverted mask is sign-extended
3337   andptr(possibly_jweak, inverted_jweak_mask);
3338 }
3339 
3340 void MacroAssembler::resolve_jobject(Register value,
3341                                      Register thread,
3342                                      Register tmp) {
3343   assert_different_registers(value, thread, tmp);
3344   Label done, not_weak;
3345   testptr(value, value);
3346   jcc(Assembler::zero, done);                // Use NULL as-is.
3347   testptr(value, JNIHandles::weak_tag_mask); // Test for jweak tag.
3348   jcc(Assembler::zero, not_weak);
3349   // Resolve jweak.
3350   access_load_at(T_OBJECT, IN_NATIVE | ON_PHANTOM_OOP_REF,
3351                  value, Address(value, -JNIHandles::weak_tag_value), tmp, thread);
3352   verify_oop(value);
3353   jmp(done);
3354   bind(not_weak);
3355   // Resolve (untagged) jobject.
3356   access_load_at(T_OBJECT, IN_NATIVE, value, Address(value, 0), tmp, thread);
3357   verify_oop(value);
3358   bind(done);
3359 }
3360 
3361 void MacroAssembler::subptr(Register dst, int32_t imm32) {
3362   LP64_ONLY(subq(dst, imm32)) NOT_LP64(subl(dst, imm32));
3363 }
3364 
3365 // Force generation of a 4 byte immediate value even if it fits into 8bit
3366 void MacroAssembler::subptr_imm32(Register dst, int32_t imm32) {
3367   LP64_ONLY(subq_imm32(dst, imm32)) NOT_LP64(subl_imm32(dst, imm32));
3368 }
3369 
3370 void MacroAssembler::subptr(Register dst, Register src) {
3371   LP64_ONLY(subq(dst, src)) NOT_LP64(subl(dst, src));
3372 }
3373 
3374 // C++ bool manipulation
3375 void MacroAssembler::testbool(Register dst) {
3376   if(sizeof(bool) == 1)
3377     testb(dst, 0xff);
3378   else if(sizeof(bool) == 2) {
3379     // testw implementation needed for two byte bools
3380     ShouldNotReachHere();
3381   } else if(sizeof(bool) == 4)
3382     testl(dst, dst);
3383   else
3384     // unsupported
3385     ShouldNotReachHere();
3386 }
3387 
3388 void MacroAssembler::testptr(Register dst, Register src) {
3389   LP64_ONLY(testq(dst, src)) NOT_LP64(testl(dst, src));
3390 }
3391 
3392 // Object / value buffer allocation...
3393 //
3394 // Kills klass and rsi on LP64
3395 void MacroAssembler::allocate_instance(Register klass, Register new_obj,
3396                                        Register t1, Register t2,
3397                                        bool clear_fields, Label& alloc_failed)
3398 {
3399   Label done, initialize_header, initialize_object, slow_case, slow_case_no_pop;
3400   Register layout_size = t1;
3401   assert(new_obj == rax, "needs to be rax, according to barrier asm eden_allocate");
3402   assert_different_registers(klass, new_obj, t1, t2);
3403 
3404 #ifdef ASSERT
3405   {
3406     Label L;
3407     cmpb(Address(klass, InstanceKlass::init_state_offset()), InstanceKlass::fully_initialized);
3408     jcc(Assembler::equal, L);
3409     stop("klass not initialized");
3410     bind(L);
3411   }
3412 #endif
3413 
3414   // get instance_size in InstanceKlass (scaled to a count of bytes)
3415   movl(layout_size, Address(klass, Klass::layout_helper_offset()));
3416   // test to see if it has a finalizer or is malformed in some way
3417   testl(layout_size, Klass::_lh_instance_slow_path_bit);
3418   jcc(Assembler::notZero, slow_case_no_pop);
3419 
3420   // Allocate the instance:
3421   //  If TLAB is enabled:
3422   //    Try to allocate in the TLAB.
3423   //    If fails, go to the slow path.
3424   //  Else If inline contiguous allocations are enabled:
3425   //    Try to allocate in eden.
3426   //    If fails due to heap end, go to slow path.
3427   //
3428   //  If TLAB is enabled OR inline contiguous is enabled:
3429   //    Initialize the allocation.
3430   //    Exit.
3431   //
3432   //  Go to slow path.
3433   const bool allow_shared_alloc =
3434     Universe::heap()->supports_inline_contig_alloc();
3435 
3436   push(klass);
3437   const Register thread = LP64_ONLY(r15_thread) NOT_LP64(klass);
3438 #ifndef _LP64
3439   if (UseTLAB || allow_shared_alloc) {
3440     get_thread(thread);
3441   }
3442 #endif // _LP64
3443 
3444   if (UseTLAB) {
3445     tlab_allocate(thread, new_obj, layout_size, 0, klass, t2, slow_case);
3446     if (ZeroTLAB || (!clear_fields)) {
3447       // the fields have been already cleared
3448       jmp(initialize_header);
3449     } else {
3450       // initialize both the header and fields
3451       jmp(initialize_object);
3452     }
3453   } else {
3454     // Allocation in the shared Eden, if allowed.
3455     //
3456     eden_allocate(thread, new_obj, layout_size, 0, t2, slow_case);
3457   }
3458 
3459   // If UseTLAB or allow_shared_alloc are true, the object is created above and
3460   // there is an initialize need. Otherwise, skip and go to the slow path.
3461   if (UseTLAB || allow_shared_alloc) {
3462     if (clear_fields) {
3463       // The object is initialized before the header.  If the object size is
3464       // zero, go directly to the header initialization.
3465       bind(initialize_object);
3466       decrement(layout_size, sizeof(oopDesc));
3467       jcc(Assembler::zero, initialize_header);
3468 
3469       // Initialize topmost object field, divide size by 8, check if odd and
3470       // test if zero.
3471       Register zero = klass;
3472       xorl(zero, zero);    // use zero reg to clear memory (shorter code)
3473       shrl(layout_size, LogBytesPerLong); // divide by 2*oopSize and set carry flag if odd
3474 
3475   #ifdef ASSERT
3476       // make sure instance_size was multiple of 8
3477       Label L;
3478       // Ignore partial flag stall after shrl() since it is debug VM
3479       jcc(Assembler::carryClear, L);
3480       stop("object size is not multiple of 2 - adjust this code");
3481       bind(L);
3482       // must be > 0, no extra check needed here
3483   #endif
3484 
3485       // initialize remaining object fields: instance_size was a multiple of 8
3486       {
3487         Label loop;
3488         bind(loop);
3489         movptr(Address(new_obj, layout_size, Address::times_8, sizeof(oopDesc) - 1*oopSize), zero);
3490         NOT_LP64(movptr(Address(new_obj, layout_size, Address::times_8, sizeof(oopDesc) - 2*oopSize), zero));
3491         decrement(layout_size);
3492         jcc(Assembler::notZero, loop);
3493       }
3494     } // clear_fields
3495 
3496     // initialize object header only.
3497     bind(initialize_header);
3498     pop(klass);
3499     Register mark_word = t2;
3500     movptr(mark_word, Address(klass, Klass::prototype_header_offset()));
3501     movptr(Address(new_obj, oopDesc::mark_offset_in_bytes ()), mark_word);
3502 #ifdef _LP64
3503     xorl(rsi, rsi);                 // use zero reg to clear memory (shorter code)
3504     store_klass_gap(new_obj, rsi);  // zero klass gap for compressed oops
3505 #endif
3506     movptr(t2, klass);         // preserve klass
3507     store_klass(new_obj, t2);  // src klass reg is potentially compressed
3508 
3509     jmp(done);
3510   }
3511 
3512   bind(slow_case);
3513   pop(klass);
3514   bind(slow_case_no_pop);
3515   jmp(alloc_failed);
3516 
3517   bind(done);
3518 }
3519 
3520 // Defines obj, preserves var_size_in_bytes, okay for t2 == var_size_in_bytes.
3521 void MacroAssembler::tlab_allocate(Register thread, Register obj,
3522                                    Register var_size_in_bytes,
3523                                    int con_size_in_bytes,
3524                                    Register t1,
3525                                    Register t2,
3526                                    Label& slow_case) {
3527   BarrierSetAssembler* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_assembler();
3528   bs->tlab_allocate(this, thread, obj, var_size_in_bytes, con_size_in_bytes, t1, t2, slow_case);
3529 }
3530 
3531 // Defines obj, preserves var_size_in_bytes
3532 void MacroAssembler::eden_allocate(Register thread, Register obj,
3533                                    Register var_size_in_bytes,
3534                                    int con_size_in_bytes,
3535                                    Register t1,
3536                                    Label& slow_case) {
3537   BarrierSetAssembler* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_assembler();
3538   bs->eden_allocate(this, thread, obj, var_size_in_bytes, con_size_in_bytes, t1, slow_case);
3539 }
3540 
3541 // Preserves the contents of address, destroys the contents length_in_bytes and temp.
3542 void MacroAssembler::zero_memory(Register address, Register length_in_bytes, int offset_in_bytes, Register temp) {
3543   assert(address != length_in_bytes && address != temp && temp != length_in_bytes, "registers must be different");
3544   assert((offset_in_bytes & (BytesPerWord - 1)) == 0, "offset must be a multiple of BytesPerWord");
3545   Label done;
3546 
3547   testptr(length_in_bytes, length_in_bytes);
3548   jcc(Assembler::zero, done);
3549 
3550   // initialize topmost word, divide index by 2, check if odd and test if zero
3551   // note: for the remaining code to work, index must be a multiple of BytesPerWord
3552 #ifdef ASSERT
3553   {
3554     Label L;
3555     testptr(length_in_bytes, BytesPerWord - 1);
3556     jcc(Assembler::zero, L);
3557     stop("length must be a multiple of BytesPerWord");
3558     bind(L);
3559   }
3560 #endif
3561   Register index = length_in_bytes;
3562   xorptr(temp, temp);    // use _zero reg to clear memory (shorter code)
3563   if (UseIncDec) {
3564     shrptr(index, 3);  // divide by 8/16 and set carry flag if bit 2 was set
3565   } else {
3566     shrptr(index, 2);  // use 2 instructions to avoid partial flag stall
3567     shrptr(index, 1);
3568   }
3569 #ifndef _LP64
3570   // index could have not been a multiple of 8 (i.e., bit 2 was set)
3571   {
3572     Label even;
3573     // note: if index was a multiple of 8, then it cannot
3574     //       be 0 now otherwise it must have been 0 before
3575     //       => if it is even, we don't need to check for 0 again
3576     jcc(Assembler::carryClear, even);
3577     // clear topmost word (no jump would be needed if conditional assignment worked here)
3578     movptr(Address(address, index, Address::times_8, offset_in_bytes - 0*BytesPerWord), temp);
3579     // index could be 0 now, must check again
3580     jcc(Assembler::zero, done);
3581     bind(even);
3582   }
3583 #endif // !_LP64
3584   // initialize remaining object fields: index is a multiple of 2 now
3585   {
3586     Label loop;
3587     bind(loop);
3588     movptr(Address(address, index, Address::times_8, offset_in_bytes - 1*BytesPerWord), temp);
3589     NOT_LP64(movptr(Address(address, index, Address::times_8, offset_in_bytes - 2*BytesPerWord), temp);)
3590     decrement(index);
3591     jcc(Assembler::notZero, loop);
3592   }
3593 
3594   bind(done);
3595 }
3596 
3597 void MacroAssembler::get_value_field_klass(Register klass, Register index, Register value_klass) {
3598   movptr(value_klass, Address(klass, InstanceKlass::value_field_klasses_offset()));
3599 #ifdef ASSERT
3600   {
3601     Label done;
3602     cmpptr(value_klass, 0);
3603     jcc(Assembler::notEqual, done);
3604     stop("get_value_field_klass contains no inline klasses");
3605     bind(done);
3606   }
3607 #endif
3608   movptr(value_klass, Address(value_klass, index, Address::times_ptr));
3609 }
3610 
3611 void MacroAssembler::get_default_value_oop(Register value_klass, Register temp_reg, Register obj) {
3612 #ifdef ASSERT
3613   {
3614     Label done_check;
3615     test_klass_is_value(value_klass, temp_reg, done_check);
3616     stop("get_default_value_oop from non-value klass");
3617     bind(done_check);
3618   }
3619 #endif
3620   Register offset = temp_reg;
3621   // Getting the offset of the pre-allocated default value
3622   movptr(offset, Address(value_klass, in_bytes(InstanceKlass::adr_valueklass_fixed_block_offset())));
3623   movl(offset, Address(offset, in_bytes(ValueKlass::default_value_offset_offset())));
3624 
3625   // Getting the mirror
3626   movptr(obj, Address(value_klass, in_bytes(Klass::java_mirror_offset())));
3627   resolve_oop_handle(obj, value_klass);
3628 
3629   // Getting the pre-allocated default value from the mirror
3630   Address field(obj, offset, Address::times_1);
3631   load_heap_oop(obj, field);
3632 }
3633 
3634 void MacroAssembler::get_empty_value_oop(Register value_klass, Register temp_reg, Register obj) {
3635 #ifdef ASSERT
3636   {
3637     Label done_check;
3638     test_klass_is_empty_value(value_klass, temp_reg, done_check);
3639     stop("get_empty_value from non-empty value klass");
3640     bind(done_check);
3641   }
3642 #endif
3643   get_default_value_oop(value_klass, temp_reg, obj);
3644 }

3646 
3647 // Look up the method for a megamorphic invokeinterface call.
3648 // The target method is determined by <intf_klass, itable_index>.
3649 // The receiver klass is in recv_klass.
3650 // On success, the result will be in method_result, and execution falls through.
3651 // On failure, execution transfers to the given label.
3652 void MacroAssembler::lookup_interface_method(Register recv_klass,
3653                                              Register intf_klass,
3654                                              RegisterOrConstant itable_index,
3655                                              Register method_result,
3656                                              Register scan_temp,
3657                                              Label& L_no_such_interface,
3658                                              bool return_method) {
3659   assert_different_registers(recv_klass, intf_klass, scan_temp);
3660   assert_different_registers(method_result, intf_klass, scan_temp);
3661   assert(recv_klass != method_result || !return_method,
3662          "recv_klass can be destroyed when method isn't needed");
3663 
3664   assert(itable_index.is_constant() || itable_index.as_register() == method_result,
3665          "caller must use same register for non-constant itable index as for method");
3666 
3667   // Compute start of first itableOffsetEntry (which is at the end of the vtable)
3668   int vtable_base = in_bytes(Klass::vtable_start_offset());
3669   int itentry_off = itableMethodEntry::method_offset_in_bytes();
3670   int scan_step   = itableOffsetEntry::size() * wordSize;
3671   int vte_size    = vtableEntry::size_in_bytes();
3672   Address::ScaleFactor times_vte_scale = Address::times_ptr;
3673   assert(vte_size == wordSize, "else adjust times_vte_scale");
3674 
3675   movl(scan_temp, Address(recv_klass, Klass::vtable_length_offset()));
3676 
3677   // %%% Could store the aligned, prescaled offset in the klassoop.
3678   lea(scan_temp, Address(recv_klass, scan_temp, times_vte_scale, vtable_base));
3679 
3680   if (return_method) {
3681     // Adjust recv_klass by scaled itable_index, so we can free itable_index.
3682     assert(itableMethodEntry::size() * wordSize == wordSize, "adjust the scaling in the code below");
3683     lea(recv_klass, Address(recv_klass, itable_index, Address::times_ptr, itentry_off));
3684   }
3685 
3686   // for (scan = klass->itable(); scan->interface() != NULL; scan += scan_step) {
3687   //   if (scan->interface() == intf) {
3688   //     result = (klass + scan->offset() + itable_index);
3689   //   }
3690   // }
3691   Label search, found_method;
3692 
3693   for (int peel = 1; peel >= 0; peel--) {
3694     movptr(method_result, Address(scan_temp, itableOffsetEntry::interface_offset_in_bytes()));
3695     cmpptr(intf_klass, method_result);
3696 
3697     if (peel) {
3698       jccb(Assembler::equal, found_method);
3699     } else {
3700       jccb(Assembler::notEqual, search);
3701       // (invert the test to fall through to found_method...)
3702     }
3703 
3704     if (!peel)  break;
3705 
3706     bind(search);
3707 
3708     // Check that the previous entry is non-null.  A null entry means that
3709     // the receiver class doesn't implement the interface, and wasn't the
3710     // same as when the caller was compiled.
3711     testptr(method_result, method_result);
3712     jcc(Assembler::zero, L_no_such_interface);
3713     addptr(scan_temp, scan_step);
3714   }
3715 
3716   bind(found_method);
3717 
3718   if (return_method) {
3719     // Got a hit.
3720     movl(scan_temp, Address(scan_temp, itableOffsetEntry::offset_offset_in_bytes()));
3721     movptr(method_result, Address(recv_klass, scan_temp, Address::times_1));
3722   }
3723 }
3724 
3725 
3726 // virtual method calling
3727 void MacroAssembler::lookup_virtual_method(Register recv_klass,
3728                                            RegisterOrConstant vtable_index,
3729                                            Register method_result) {
3730   const int base = in_bytes(Klass::vtable_start_offset());
3731   assert(vtableEntry::size() * wordSize == wordSize, "else adjust the scaling in the code below");
3732   Address vtable_entry_addr(recv_klass,
3733                             vtable_index, Address::times_ptr,
3734                             base + vtableEntry::method_offset_in_bytes());
3735   movptr(method_result, vtable_entry_addr);
3736 }
3737 
3738 
3739 void MacroAssembler::check_klass_subtype(Register sub_klass,
3740                            Register super_klass,
3741                            Register temp_reg,
3742                            Label& L_success) {
3743   Label L_failure;
3744   check_klass_subtype_fast_path(sub_klass, super_klass, temp_reg,        &L_success, &L_failure, NULL);
3745   check_klass_subtype_slow_path(sub_klass, super_klass, temp_reg, noreg, &L_success, NULL);
3746   bind(L_failure);
3747 }
3748 
3749 
3750 void MacroAssembler::check_klass_subtype_fast_path(Register sub_klass,
3751                                                    Register super_klass,
3752                                                    Register temp_reg,
3753                                                    Label* L_success,
3754                                                    Label* L_failure,
3755                                                    Label* L_slow_path,
3756                                         RegisterOrConstant super_check_offset) {
3757   assert_different_registers(sub_klass, super_klass, temp_reg);
3758   bool must_load_sco = (super_check_offset.constant_or_zero() == -1);
3759   if (super_check_offset.is_register()) {
3760     assert_different_registers(sub_klass, super_klass,
3761                                super_check_offset.as_register());
3762   } else if (must_load_sco) {
3763     assert(temp_reg != noreg, "supply either a temp or a register offset");
3764   }
3765 
3766   Label L_fallthrough;
3767   int label_nulls = 0;
3768   if (L_success == NULL)   { L_success   = &L_fallthrough; label_nulls++; }
3769   if (L_failure == NULL)   { L_failure   = &L_fallthrough; label_nulls++; }
3770   if (L_slow_path == NULL) { L_slow_path = &L_fallthrough; label_nulls++; }
3771   assert(label_nulls <= 1, "at most one NULL in the batch");
3772 
3773   int sc_offset = in_bytes(Klass::secondary_super_cache_offset());
3774   int sco_offset = in_bytes(Klass::super_check_offset_offset());
3775   Address super_check_offset_addr(super_klass, sco_offset);
3776 
3777   // Hacked jcc, which "knows" that L_fallthrough, at least, is in
3778   // range of a jccb.  If this routine grows larger, reconsider at
3779   // least some of these.
3780 #define local_jcc(assembler_cond, label)                                \
3781   if (&(label) == &L_fallthrough)  jccb(assembler_cond, label);         \
3782   else                             jcc( assembler_cond, label) /*omit semi*/
3783 
3784   // Hacked jmp, which may only be used just before L_fallthrough.
3785 #define final_jmp(label)                                                \
3786   if (&(label) == &L_fallthrough) { /*do nothing*/ }                    \
3787   else                            jmp(label)                /*omit semi*/
3788 
3789   // If the pointers are equal, we are done (e.g., String[] elements).
3790   // This self-check enables sharing of secondary supertype arrays among
3791   // non-primary types such as array-of-interface.  Otherwise, each such
3792   // type would need its own customized SSA.
3793   // We move this check to the front of the fast path because many
3794   // type checks are in fact trivially successful in this manner,
3795   // so we get a nicely predicted branch right at the start of the check.
3796   cmpptr(sub_klass, super_klass);
3797   local_jcc(Assembler::equal, *L_success);
3798 
3799   // Check the supertype display:
3800   if (must_load_sco) {
3801     // Positive movl does right thing on LP64.
3802     movl(temp_reg, super_check_offset_addr);
3803     super_check_offset = RegisterOrConstant(temp_reg);
3804   }
3805   Address super_check_addr(sub_klass, super_check_offset, Address::times_1, 0);
3806   cmpptr(super_klass, super_check_addr); // load displayed supertype
3807 
3808   // This check has worked decisively for primary supers.
3809   // Secondary supers are sought in the super_cache ('super_cache_addr').
3810   // (Secondary supers are interfaces and very deeply nested subtypes.)
3811   // This works in the same check above because of a tricky aliasing
3812   // between the super_cache and the primary super display elements.
3813   // (The 'super_check_addr' can address either, as the case requires.)
3814   // Note that the cache is updated below if it does not help us find
3815   // what we need immediately.
3816   // So if it was a primary super, we can just fail immediately.
3817   // Otherwise, it's the slow path for us (no success at this point).
3818 
3819   if (super_check_offset.is_register()) {
3820     local_jcc(Assembler::equal, *L_success);
3821     cmpl(super_check_offset.as_register(), sc_offset);
3822     if (L_failure == &L_fallthrough) {
3823       local_jcc(Assembler::equal, *L_slow_path);
3824     } else {
3825       local_jcc(Assembler::notEqual, *L_failure);
3826       final_jmp(*L_slow_path);
3827     }
3828   } else if (super_check_offset.as_constant() == sc_offset) {
3829     // Need a slow path; fast failure is impossible.
3830     if (L_slow_path == &L_fallthrough) {
3831       local_jcc(Assembler::equal, *L_success);
3832     } else {
3833       local_jcc(Assembler::notEqual, *L_slow_path);
3834       final_jmp(*L_success);
3835     }
3836   } else {
3837     // No slow path; it's a fast decision.
3838     if (L_failure == &L_fallthrough) {
3839       local_jcc(Assembler::equal, *L_success);
3840     } else {
3841       local_jcc(Assembler::notEqual, *L_failure);
3842       final_jmp(*L_success);
3843     }
3844   }
3845 
3846   bind(L_fallthrough);
3847 
3848 #undef local_jcc
3849 #undef final_jmp
3850 }
3851 
3852 
3853 void MacroAssembler::check_klass_subtype_slow_path(Register sub_klass,
3854                                                    Register super_klass,
3855                                                    Register temp_reg,
3856                                                    Register temp2_reg,
3857                                                    Label* L_success,
3858                                                    Label* L_failure,
3859                                                    bool set_cond_codes) {
3860   assert_different_registers(sub_klass, super_klass, temp_reg);
3861   if (temp2_reg != noreg)
3862     assert_different_registers(sub_klass, super_klass, temp_reg, temp2_reg);
3863 #define IS_A_TEMP(reg) ((reg) == temp_reg || (reg) == temp2_reg)
3864 
3865   Label L_fallthrough;
3866   int label_nulls = 0;
3867   if (L_success == NULL)   { L_success   = &L_fallthrough; label_nulls++; }
3868   if (L_failure == NULL)   { L_failure   = &L_fallthrough; label_nulls++; }
3869   assert(label_nulls <= 1, "at most one NULL in the batch");
3870 
3871   // a couple of useful fields in sub_klass:
3872   int ss_offset = in_bytes(Klass::secondary_supers_offset());
3873   int sc_offset = in_bytes(Klass::secondary_super_cache_offset());
3874   Address secondary_supers_addr(sub_klass, ss_offset);
3875   Address super_cache_addr(     sub_klass, sc_offset);
3876 
3877   // Do a linear scan of the secondary super-klass chain.
3878   // This code is rarely used, so simplicity is a virtue here.
3879   // The repne_scan instruction uses fixed registers, which we must spill.
3880   // Don't worry too much about pre-existing connections with the input regs.
3881 
3882   assert(sub_klass != rax, "killed reg"); // killed by mov(rax, super)
3883   assert(sub_klass != rcx, "killed reg"); // killed by lea(rcx, &pst_counter)
3884 
3885   // Get super_klass value into rax (even if it was in rdi or rcx).
3886   bool pushed_rax = false, pushed_rcx = false, pushed_rdi = false;
3887   if (super_klass != rax || UseCompressedOops) {
3888     if (!IS_A_TEMP(rax)) { push(rax); pushed_rax = true; }
3889     mov(rax, super_klass);
3890   }
3891   if (!IS_A_TEMP(rcx)) { push(rcx); pushed_rcx = true; }
3892   if (!IS_A_TEMP(rdi)) { push(rdi); pushed_rdi = true; }
3893 
3894 #ifndef PRODUCT
3895   int* pst_counter = &SharedRuntime::_partial_subtype_ctr;
3896   ExternalAddress pst_counter_addr((address) pst_counter);
3897   NOT_LP64(  incrementl(pst_counter_addr) );
3898   LP64_ONLY( lea(rcx, pst_counter_addr) );
3899   LP64_ONLY( incrementl(Address(rcx, 0)) );
3900 #endif //PRODUCT
3901 
3902   // We will consult the secondary-super array.
3903   movptr(rdi, secondary_supers_addr);
3904   // Load the array length.  (Positive movl does right thing on LP64.)
3905   movl(rcx, Address(rdi, Array<Klass*>::length_offset_in_bytes()));
3906   // Skip to start of data.
3907   addptr(rdi, Array<Klass*>::base_offset_in_bytes());
3908 
3909   // Scan RCX words at [RDI] for an occurrence of RAX.
3910   // Set NZ/Z based on last compare.
3911   // Z flag value will not be set by 'repne' if RCX == 0 since 'repne' does
3912   // not change flags (only scas instruction which is repeated sets flags).
3913   // Set Z = 0 (not equal) before 'repne' to indicate that class was not found.
3914 
3915     testptr(rax,rax); // Set Z = 0
3916     repne_scan();
3917 
3918   // Unspill the temp. registers:
3919   if (pushed_rdi)  pop(rdi);
3920   if (pushed_rcx)  pop(rcx);
3921   if (pushed_rax)  pop(rax);
3922 
3923   if (set_cond_codes) {
3924     // Special hack for the AD files:  rdi is guaranteed non-zero.
3925     assert(!pushed_rdi, "rdi must be left non-NULL");
3926     // Also, the condition codes are properly set Z/NZ on succeed/failure.
3927   }
3928 
3929   if (L_failure == &L_fallthrough)
3930         jccb(Assembler::notEqual, *L_failure);
3931   else  jcc(Assembler::notEqual, *L_failure);
3932 
3933   // Success.  Cache the super we found and proceed in triumph.
3934   movptr(super_cache_addr, super_klass);
3935 
3936   if (L_success != &L_fallthrough) {
3937     jmp(*L_success);
3938   }
3939 
3940 #undef IS_A_TEMP
3941 
3942   bind(L_fallthrough);
3943 }
3944 
3945 void MacroAssembler::clinit_barrier(Register klass, Register thread, Label* L_fast_path, Label* L_slow_path) {
3946   assert(L_fast_path != NULL || L_slow_path != NULL, "at least one is required");
3947 
3948   Label L_fallthrough;
3949   if (L_fast_path == NULL) {
3950     L_fast_path = &L_fallthrough;
3951   } else if (L_slow_path == NULL) {
3952     L_slow_path = &L_fallthrough;
3953   }
3954 
3955   // Fast path check: class is fully initialized
3956   cmpb(Address(klass, InstanceKlass::init_state_offset()), InstanceKlass::fully_initialized);
3957   jcc(Assembler::equal, *L_fast_path);
3958 
3959   // Fast path check: current thread is initializer thread
3960   cmpptr(thread, Address(klass, InstanceKlass::init_thread_offset()));
3961   if (L_slow_path == &L_fallthrough) {
3962     jcc(Assembler::equal, *L_fast_path);
3963     bind(*L_slow_path);
3964   } else if (L_fast_path == &L_fallthrough) {
3965     jcc(Assembler::notEqual, *L_slow_path);
3966     bind(*L_fast_path);
3967   } else {
3968     Unimplemented();
3969   }
3970 }
3971 
3972 void MacroAssembler::cmov32(Condition cc, Register dst, Address src) {
3973   if (VM_Version::supports_cmov()) {
3974     cmovl(cc, dst, src);
3975   } else {
3976     Label L;
3977     jccb(negate_condition(cc), L);
3978     movl(dst, src);
3979     bind(L);
3980   }
3981 }
3982 
3983 void MacroAssembler::cmov32(Condition cc, Register dst, Register src) {
3984   if (VM_Version::supports_cmov()) {
3985     cmovl(cc, dst, src);
3986   } else {
3987     Label L;
3988     jccb(negate_condition(cc), L);
3989     movl(dst, src);
3990     bind(L);
3991   }
3992 }
3993 
3994 void MacroAssembler::_verify_oop(Register reg, const char* s, const char* file, int line) {
3995   if (!VerifyOops || VerifyAdapterSharing) {
3996     // Below address of the code string confuses VerifyAdapterSharing
3997     // because it may differ between otherwise equivalent adapters.
3998     return;
3999   }
4000 
4001   // Pass register number to verify_oop_subroutine
4002   const char* b = NULL;
4003   {
4004     ResourceMark rm;
4005     stringStream ss;
4006     ss.print("verify_oop: %s: %s (%s:%d)", reg->name(), s, file, line);
4007     b = code_string(ss.as_string());
4008   }
4009   BLOCK_COMMENT("verify_oop {");
4010 #ifdef _LP64
4011   push(rscratch1);                    // save r10, trashed by movptr()
4012 #endif
4013   push(rax);                          // save rax,
4014   push(reg);                          // pass register argument
4015   ExternalAddress buffer((address) b);
4016   // avoid using pushptr, as it modifies scratch registers
4017   // and our contract is not to modify anything
4018   movptr(rax, buffer.addr());
4019   push(rax);
4020   // call indirectly to solve generation ordering problem
4021   movptr(rax, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::verify_oop_subroutine_entry_address()));
4022   call(rax);
4023   // Caller pops the arguments (oop, message) and restores rax, r10
4024   BLOCK_COMMENT("} verify_oop");
4025 }
4026 
4027 
4028 RegisterOrConstant MacroAssembler::delayed_value_impl(intptr_t* delayed_value_addr,
4029                                                       Register tmp,
4030                                                       int offset) {
4031   intptr_t value = *delayed_value_addr;
4032   if (value != 0)
4033     return RegisterOrConstant(value + offset);
4034 
4035   // load indirectly to solve generation ordering problem
4036   movptr(tmp, ExternalAddress((address) delayed_value_addr));
4037 
4038 #ifdef ASSERT
4039   { Label L;
4040     testptr(tmp, tmp);
4041     if (WizardMode) {
4042       const char* buf = NULL;
4043       {
4044         ResourceMark rm;
4045         stringStream ss;
4046         ss.print("DelayedValue=" INTPTR_FORMAT, delayed_value_addr[1]);
4047         buf = code_string(ss.as_string());
4048       }
4049       jcc(Assembler::notZero, L);
4050       STOP(buf);
4051     } else {
4052       jccb(Assembler::notZero, L);
4053       hlt();
4054     }
4055     bind(L);
4056   }
4057 #endif
4058 
4059   if (offset != 0)
4060     addptr(tmp, offset);
4061 
4062   return RegisterOrConstant(tmp);
4063 }
4064 
4065 
4066 Address MacroAssembler::argument_address(RegisterOrConstant arg_slot,
4067                                          int extra_slot_offset) {
4068   // cf. TemplateTable::prepare_invoke(), if (load_receiver).
4069   int stackElementSize = Interpreter::stackElementSize;
4070   int offset = Interpreter::expr_offset_in_bytes(extra_slot_offset+0);
4071 #ifdef ASSERT
4072   int offset1 = Interpreter::expr_offset_in_bytes(extra_slot_offset+1);
4073   assert(offset1 - offset == stackElementSize, "correct arithmetic");
4074 #endif
4075   Register             scale_reg    = noreg;
4076   Address::ScaleFactor scale_factor = Address::no_scale;
4077   if (arg_slot.is_constant()) {
4078     offset += arg_slot.as_constant() * stackElementSize;
4079   } else {
4080     scale_reg    = arg_slot.as_register();
4081     scale_factor = Address::times(stackElementSize);
4082   }
4083   offset += wordSize;           // return PC is on stack
4084   return Address(rsp, scale_reg, scale_factor, offset);
4085 }
4086 
4087 
4088 void MacroAssembler::_verify_oop_addr(Address addr, const char* s, const char* file, int line) {
4089   if (!VerifyOops || VerifyAdapterSharing) {
4090     // Below address of the code string confuses VerifyAdapterSharing
4091     // because it may differ between otherwise equivalent adapters.
4092     return;
4093   }
4094 
4095   // Address adjust(addr.base(), addr.index(), addr.scale(), addr.disp() + BytesPerWord);
4096   // Pass register number to verify_oop_subroutine
4097   const char* b = NULL;
4098   {
4099     ResourceMark rm;
4100     stringStream ss;
4101     ss.print("verify_oop_addr: %s (%s:%d)", s, file, line);
4102     b = code_string(ss.as_string());
4103   }
4104 #ifdef _LP64
4105   push(rscratch1);                    // save r10, trashed by movptr()
4106 #endif
4107   push(rax);                          // save rax,
4108   // addr may contain rsp so we will have to adjust it based on the push
4109   // we just did (and on 64 bit we do two pushes)
4110   // NOTE: 64bit seemed to have had a bug in that it did movq(addr, rax); which
4111   // stores rax into addr which is backwards of what was intended.
4112   if (addr.uses(rsp)) {
4113     lea(rax, addr);
4114     pushptr(Address(rax, LP64_ONLY(2 *) BytesPerWord));
4115   } else {
4116     pushptr(addr);
4117   }
4118 
4119   ExternalAddress buffer((address) b);
4120   // pass msg argument
4121   // avoid using pushptr, as it modifies scratch registers
4122   // and our contract is not to modify anything
4123   movptr(rax, buffer.addr());
4124   push(rax);
4125 
4126   // call indirectly to solve generation ordering problem
4127   movptr(rax, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::verify_oop_subroutine_entry_address()));
4128   call(rax);
4129   // Caller pops the arguments (addr, message) and restores rax, r10.
4130 }
4131 
4132 void MacroAssembler::verify_tlab() {
4133 #ifdef ASSERT
4134   if (UseTLAB && VerifyOops) {
4135     Label next, ok;
4136     Register t1 = rsi;
4137     Register thread_reg = NOT_LP64(rbx) LP64_ONLY(r15_thread);
4138 
4139     push(t1);
4140     NOT_LP64(push(thread_reg));
4141     NOT_LP64(get_thread(thread_reg));
4142 
4143     movptr(t1, Address(thread_reg, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_top_offset())));
4144     cmpptr(t1, Address(thread_reg, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_start_offset())));
4145     jcc(Assembler::aboveEqual, next);
4146     STOP("assert(top >= start)");
4147     should_not_reach_here();
4148 
4149     bind(next);
4150     movptr(t1, Address(thread_reg, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_end_offset())));
4151     cmpptr(t1, Address(thread_reg, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_top_offset())));
4152     jcc(Assembler::aboveEqual, ok);
4153     STOP("assert(top <= end)");
4154     should_not_reach_here();
4155 
4156     bind(ok);
4157     NOT_LP64(pop(thread_reg));
4158     pop(t1);
4159   }
4160 #endif
4161 }
4162 
4163 class ControlWord {
4164  public:
4165   int32_t _value;
4166 
4167   int  rounding_control() const        { return  (_value >> 10) & 3      ; }
4168   int  precision_control() const       { return  (_value >>  8) & 3      ; }
4169   bool precision() const               { return ((_value >>  5) & 1) != 0; }
4170   bool underflow() const               { return ((_value >>  4) & 1) != 0; }
4171   bool overflow() const                { return ((_value >>  3) & 1) != 0; }
4172   bool zero_divide() const             { return ((_value >>  2) & 1) != 0; }
4173   bool denormalized() const            { return ((_value >>  1) & 1) != 0; }
4174   bool invalid() const                 { return ((_value >>  0) & 1) != 0; }
4175 
4176   void print() const {
4177     // rounding control
4178     const char* rc;
4179     switch (rounding_control()) {
4180       case 0: rc = "round near"; break;
4181       case 1: rc = "round down"; break;
4182       case 2: rc = "round up  "; break;
4183       case 3: rc = "chop      "; break;
4184     };
4185     // precision control
4186     const char* pc;
4187     switch (precision_control()) {
4188       case 0: pc = "24 bits "; break;
4189       case 1: pc = "reserved"; break;
4190       case 2: pc = "53 bits "; break;
4191       case 3: pc = "64 bits "; break;
4192     };
4193     // flags
4194     char f[9];
4195     f[0] = ' ';
4196     f[1] = ' ';
4197     f[2] = (precision   ()) ? 'P' : 'p';
4198     f[3] = (underflow   ()) ? 'U' : 'u';
4199     f[4] = (overflow    ()) ? 'O' : 'o';
4200     f[5] = (zero_divide ()) ? 'Z' : 'z';
4201     f[6] = (denormalized()) ? 'D' : 'd';
4202     f[7] = (invalid     ()) ? 'I' : 'i';
4203     f[8] = '\x0';
4204     // output
4205     printf("%04x  masks = %s, %s, %s", _value & 0xFFFF, f, rc, pc);
4206   }
4207 
4208 };
4209 
4210 class StatusWord {
4211  public:
4212   int32_t _value;
4213 
4214   bool busy() const                    { return ((_value >> 15) & 1) != 0; }
4215   bool C3() const                      { return ((_value >> 14) & 1) != 0; }
4216   bool C2() const                      { return ((_value >> 10) & 1) != 0; }
4217   bool C1() const                      { return ((_value >>  9) & 1) != 0; }
4218   bool C0() const                      { return ((_value >>  8) & 1) != 0; }
4219   int  top() const                     { return  (_value >> 11) & 7      ; }
4220   bool error_status() const            { return ((_value >>  7) & 1) != 0; }
4221   bool stack_fault() const             { return ((_value >>  6) & 1) != 0; }
4222   bool precision() const               { return ((_value >>  5) & 1) != 0; }
4223   bool underflow() const               { return ((_value >>  4) & 1) != 0; }
4224   bool overflow() const                { return ((_value >>  3) & 1) != 0; }
4225   bool zero_divide() const             { return ((_value >>  2) & 1) != 0; }
4226   bool denormalized() const            { return ((_value >>  1) & 1) != 0; }
4227   bool invalid() const                 { return ((_value >>  0) & 1) != 0; }
4228 
4229   void print() const {
4230     // condition codes
4231     char c[5];
4232     c[0] = (C3()) ? '3' : '-';
4233     c[1] = (C2()) ? '2' : '-';
4234     c[2] = (C1()) ? '1' : '-';
4235     c[3] = (C0()) ? '0' : '-';
4236     c[4] = '\x0';
4237     // flags
4238     char f[9];
4239     f[0] = (error_status()) ? 'E' : '-';
4240     f[1] = (stack_fault ()) ? 'S' : '-';
4241     f[2] = (precision   ()) ? 'P' : '-';
4242     f[3] = (underflow   ()) ? 'U' : '-';
4243     f[4] = (overflow    ()) ? 'O' : '-';
4244     f[5] = (zero_divide ()) ? 'Z' : '-';
4245     f[6] = (denormalized()) ? 'D' : '-';
4246     f[7] = (invalid     ()) ? 'I' : '-';
4247     f[8] = '\x0';
4248     // output
4249     printf("%04x  flags = %s, cc =  %s, top = %d", _value & 0xFFFF, f, c, top());
4250   }
4251 
4252 };

4254 class TagWord {
4255  public:
4256   int32_t _value;
4257 
4258   int tag_at(int i) const              { return (_value >> (i*2)) & 3; }
4259 
4260   void print() const {
4261     printf("%04x", _value & 0xFFFF);
4262   }
4263 
4264 };

4266 class FPU_Register {
4267  public:
4268   int32_t _m0;
4269   int32_t _m1;
4270   int16_t _ex;
4271 
4272   bool is_indefinite() const           {
4273     return _ex == -1 && _m1 == (int32_t)0xC0000000 && _m0 == 0;
4274   }
4275 
4276   void print() const {
4277     char  sign = (_ex < 0) ? '-' : '+';
4278     const char* kind = (_ex == 0x7FFF || _ex == (int16_t)-1) ? "NaN" : "   ";
4279     printf("%c%04hx.%08x%08x  %s", sign, _ex, _m1, _m0, kind);
4280   };
4281 
4282 };
4283 
4284 class FPU_State {
4285  public:
4286   enum {
4287     register_size       = 10,
4288     number_of_registers =  8,
4289     register_mask       =  7
4290   };
4291 
4292   ControlWord  _control_word;
4293   StatusWord   _status_word;
4294   TagWord      _tag_word;
4295   int32_t      _error_offset;
4296   int32_t      _error_selector;
4297   int32_t      _data_offset;
4298   int32_t      _data_selector;
4299   int8_t       _register[register_size * number_of_registers];
4300 
4301   int tag_for_st(int i) const          { return _tag_word.tag_at((_status_word.top() + i) & register_mask); }
4302   FPU_Register* st(int i) const        { return (FPU_Register*)&_register[register_size * i]; }
4303 
4304   const char* tag_as_string(int tag) const {
4305     switch (tag) {
4306       case 0: return "valid";
4307       case 1: return "zero";
4308       case 2: return "special";
4309       case 3: return "empty";
4310     }
4311     ShouldNotReachHere();
4312     return NULL;
4313   }
4314 
4315   void print() const {
4316     // print computation registers
4317     { int t = _status_word.top();
4318       for (int i = 0; i < number_of_registers; i++) {
4319         int j = (i - t) & register_mask;
4320         printf("%c r%d = ST%d = ", (j == 0 ? '*' : ' '), i, j);
4321         st(j)->print();
4322         printf(" %s\n", tag_as_string(_tag_word.tag_at(i)));
4323       }
4324     }
4325     printf("\n");
4326     // print control registers
4327     printf("ctrl = "); _control_word.print(); printf("\n");
4328     printf("stat = "); _status_word .print(); printf("\n");
4329     printf("tags = "); _tag_word    .print(); printf("\n");
4330   }
4331 
4332 };

4334 class Flag_Register {
4335  public:
4336   int32_t _value;
4337 
4338   bool overflow() const                { return ((_value >> 11) & 1) != 0; }
4339   bool direction() const               { return ((_value >> 10) & 1) != 0; }
4340   bool sign() const                    { return ((_value >>  7) & 1) != 0; }
4341   bool zero() const                    { return ((_value >>  6) & 1) != 0; }
4342   bool auxiliary_carry() const         { return ((_value >>  4) & 1) != 0; }
4343   bool parity() const                  { return ((_value >>  2) & 1) != 0; }
4344   bool carry() const                   { return ((_value >>  0) & 1) != 0; }
4345 
4346   void print() const {
4347     // flags
4348     char f[8];
4349     f[0] = (overflow       ()) ? 'O' : '-';
4350     f[1] = (direction      ()) ? 'D' : '-';
4351     f[2] = (sign           ()) ? 'S' : '-';
4352     f[3] = (zero           ()) ? 'Z' : '-';
4353     f[4] = (auxiliary_carry()) ? 'A' : '-';
4354     f[5] = (parity         ()) ? 'P' : '-';
4355     f[6] = (carry          ()) ? 'C' : '-';
4356     f[7] = '\x0';
4357     // output
4358     printf("%08x  flags = %s", _value, f);
4359   }
4360 
4361 };

4418 static void _print_CPU_state(CPU_State* state) {

4421 
4422 
4423 void MacroAssembler::print_CPU_state() {
4424   push_CPU_state();
4425   push(rsp);                // pass CPU state
4426   call(RuntimeAddress(CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, _print_CPU_state)));
4427   addptr(rsp, wordSize);       // discard argument
4428   pop_CPU_state();
4429 }
4430 
4431 
4432 #ifndef _LP64
4433 static bool _verify_FPU(int stack_depth, char* s, CPU_State* state) {
4434   static int counter = 0;
4435   FPU_State* fs = &state->_fpu_state;
4436   counter++;
4437   // For leaf calls, only verify that the top few elements remain empty.
4438   // We only need 1 empty at the top for C2 code.
4439   if( stack_depth < 0 ) {
4440     if( fs->tag_for_st(7) != 3 ) {
4441       printf("FPR7 not empty\n");
4442       state->print();
4443       assert(false, "error");
4444       return false;
4445     }
4446     return true;                // All other stack states do not matter
4447   }
4448 
4449   assert((fs->_control_word._value & 0xffff) == StubRoutines::_fpu_cntrl_wrd_std,
4450          "bad FPU control word");
4451 
4452   // compute stack depth
4453   int i = 0;
4454   while (i < FPU_State::number_of_registers && fs->tag_for_st(i)  < 3) i++;
4455   int d = i;
4456   while (i < FPU_State::number_of_registers && fs->tag_for_st(i) == 3) i++;
4457   // verify findings
4458   if (i != FPU_State::number_of_registers) {
4459     // stack not contiguous
4460     printf("%s: stack not contiguous at ST%d\n", s, i);
4461     state->print();
4462     assert(false, "error");
4463     return false;
4464   }
4465   // check if computed stack depth corresponds to expected stack depth
4466   if (stack_depth < 0) {
4467     // expected stack depth is -stack_depth or less
4468     if (d > -stack_depth) {
4469       // too many elements on the stack
4470       printf("%s: <= %d stack elements expected but found %d\n", s, -stack_depth, d);
4471       state->print();
4472       assert(false, "error");
4473       return false;
4474     }
4475   } else {
4476     // expected stack depth is stack_depth
4477     if (d != stack_depth) {
4478       // wrong stack depth
4479       printf("%s: %d stack elements expected but found %d\n", s, stack_depth, d);
4480       state->print();
4481       assert(false, "error");
4482       return false;
4483     }
4484   }
4485   // everything is cool
4486   return true;
4487 }
4488 
4489 void MacroAssembler::verify_FPU(int stack_depth, const char* s) {
4490   if (!VerifyFPU) return;
4491   push_CPU_state();
4492   push(rsp);                // pass CPU state
4493   ExternalAddress msg((address) s);
4494   // pass message string s
4495   pushptr(msg.addr());
4496   push(stack_depth);        // pass stack depth
4497   call(RuntimeAddress(CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, _verify_FPU)));
4498   addptr(rsp, 3 * wordSize);   // discard arguments
4499   // check for error
4500   { Label L;
4501     testl(rax, rax);
4502     jcc(Assembler::notZero, L);
4503     int3();                  // break if error condition
4504     bind(L);
4505   }
4506   pop_CPU_state();
4507 }
4508 #endif // _LP64
4509 
4510 void MacroAssembler::restore_cpu_control_state_after_jni() {
4511   // Either restore the MXCSR register after returning from the JNI Call
4512   // or verify that it wasn't changed (with -Xcheck:jni flag).
4513   if (VM_Version::supports_sse()) {
4514     if (RestoreMXCSROnJNICalls) {
4515       ldmxcsr(ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::addr_mxcsr_std()));
4516     } else if (CheckJNICalls) {
4517       call(RuntimeAddress(StubRoutines::x86::verify_mxcsr_entry()));
4518     }
4519   }
4520   // Clear upper bits of YMM registers to avoid SSE <-> AVX transition penalty.
4521   vzeroupper();
4522   // Reset k1 to 0xffff.
4523 
4524 #ifdef COMPILER2
4525   if (PostLoopMultiversioning && VM_Version::supports_evex()) {
4526     push(rcx);
4527     movl(rcx, 0xffff);
4528     kmovwl(k1, rcx);
4529     pop(rcx);
4530   }
4531 #endif // COMPILER2
4532 
4533 #ifndef _LP64
4534   // Either restore the x87 floating pointer control word after returning
4535   // from the JNI call or verify that it wasn't changed.
4536   if (CheckJNICalls) {
4537     call(RuntimeAddress(StubRoutines::x86::verify_fpu_cntrl_wrd_entry()));
4538   }
4539 #endif // _LP64
4540 }
4541 
4542 // ((OopHandle)result).resolve();
4543 void MacroAssembler::resolve_oop_handle(Register result, Register tmp) {
4544   assert_different_registers(result, tmp);
4545 
4546   // Only 64 bit platforms support GCs that require a tmp register
4547   // Only IN_HEAP loads require a thread_tmp register
4548   // OopHandle::resolve is an indirection like jobject.
4549   access_load_at(T_OBJECT, IN_NATIVE,
4550                  result, Address(result, 0), tmp, /*tmp_thread*/noreg);
4551 }
4552 
4553 // ((WeakHandle)result).resolve();
4554 void MacroAssembler::resolve_weak_handle(Register rresult, Register rtmp) {
4555   assert_different_registers(rresult, rtmp);
4556   Label resolved;
4557 
4558   // A null weak handle resolves to null.
4559   cmpptr(rresult, 0);
4560   jcc(Assembler::equal, resolved);
4561 
4562   // Only 64 bit platforms support GCs that require a tmp register
4563   // Only IN_HEAP loads require a thread_tmp register
4564   // WeakHandle::resolve is an indirection like jweak.
4565   access_load_at(T_OBJECT, IN_NATIVE | ON_PHANTOM_OOP_REF,
4566                  rresult, Address(rresult, 0), rtmp, /*tmp_thread*/noreg);
4567   bind(resolved);
4568 }
4569 
4570 void MacroAssembler::load_mirror(Register mirror, Register method, Register tmp) {
4571   // get mirror
4572   const int mirror_offset = in_bytes(Klass::java_mirror_offset());
4573   load_method_holder(mirror, method);
4574   movptr(mirror, Address(mirror, mirror_offset));
4575   resolve_oop_handle(mirror, tmp);
4576 }
4577 
4578 void MacroAssembler::load_method_holder_cld(Register rresult, Register rmethod) {
4579   load_method_holder(rresult, rmethod);
4580   movptr(rresult, Address(rresult, InstanceKlass::class_loader_data_offset()));
4581 }
4582 
4583 void MacroAssembler::load_metadata(Register dst, Register src) {
4584   if (UseCompressedClassPointers) {
4585     movl(dst, Address(src, oopDesc::klass_offset_in_bytes()));
4586   } else {
4587     movptr(dst, Address(src, oopDesc::klass_offset_in_bytes()));
4588   }
4589 }
4590 
4591 void MacroAssembler::load_storage_props(Register dst, Register src) {
4592   load_metadata(dst, src);
4593   if (UseCompressedClassPointers) {
4594     shrl(dst, oopDesc::narrow_storage_props_shift);
4595   } else {
4596     shrq(dst, oopDesc::wide_storage_props_shift);
4597   }
4598 }
4599 
4600 void MacroAssembler::load_method_holder(Register holder, Register method) {
4601   movptr(holder, Address(method, Method::const_offset()));                      // ConstMethod*
4602   movptr(holder, Address(holder, ConstMethod::constants_offset()));             // ConstantPool*
4603   movptr(holder, Address(holder, ConstantPool::pool_holder_offset_in_bytes())); // InstanceKlass*
4604 }
4605 
4606 void MacroAssembler::load_klass(Register dst, Register src) {
4607   load_metadata(dst, src);
4608 #ifdef _LP64
4609   if (UseCompressedClassPointers) {
4610     andl(dst, oopDesc::compressed_klass_mask());
4611     decode_klass_not_null(dst);
4612   } else
4613 #endif
4614   {
4615 #ifdef _LP64
4616     shlq(dst, oopDesc::storage_props_nof_bits);
4617     shrq(dst, oopDesc::storage_props_nof_bits);
4618 #else
4619     andl(dst, oopDesc::wide_klass_mask());
4620 #endif
4621   }
4622 }
4623 
4624 void MacroAssembler::load_prototype_header(Register dst, Register src) {
4625   load_klass(dst, src);
4626   movptr(dst, Address(dst, Klass::prototype_header_offset()));
4627 }
4628 
4629 void MacroAssembler::store_klass(Register dst, Register src) {
4630 #ifdef _LP64
4631   if (UseCompressedClassPointers) {
4632     encode_klass_not_null(src);
4633     movl(Address(dst, oopDesc::klass_offset_in_bytes()), src);
4634   } else
4635 #endif
4636     movptr(Address(dst, oopDesc::klass_offset_in_bytes()), src);
4637 }
4638 
4639 void MacroAssembler::access_load_at(BasicType type, DecoratorSet decorators, Register dst, Address src,
4640                                     Register tmp1, Register thread_tmp) {
4641   BarrierSetAssembler* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_assembler();
4642   decorators = AccessInternal::decorator_fixup(decorators);
4643   bool as_raw = (decorators & AS_RAW) != 0;
4644   if (as_raw) {
4645     bs->BarrierSetAssembler::load_at(this, decorators, type, dst, src, tmp1, thread_tmp);
4646   } else {
4647     bs->load_at(this, decorators, type, dst, src, tmp1, thread_tmp);
4648   }
4649 }
4650 
4651 void MacroAssembler::access_store_at(BasicType type, DecoratorSet decorators, Address dst, Register src,
4652                                      Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3) {
4653   BarrierSetAssembler* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_assembler();
4654   decorators = AccessInternal::decorator_fixup(decorators);
4655   bool as_raw = (decorators & AS_RAW) != 0;
4656   if (as_raw) {
4657     bs->BarrierSetAssembler::store_at(this, decorators, type, dst, src, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3);
4658   } else {
4659     bs->store_at(this, decorators, type, dst, src, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3);
4660   }
4661 }
4662 
4663 void MacroAssembler::access_value_copy(DecoratorSet decorators, Register src, Register dst,
4664                                        Register value_klass) {
4665   BarrierSetAssembler* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_assembler();
4666   bs->value_copy(this, decorators, src, dst, value_klass);
4667 }
4668 
4669 void MacroAssembler::first_field_offset(Register value_klass, Register offset) {
4670   movptr(offset, Address(value_klass, InstanceKlass::adr_valueklass_fixed_block_offset()));
4671   movl(offset, Address(offset, ValueKlass::first_field_offset_offset()));
4672 }
4673 
4674 void MacroAssembler::data_for_oop(Register oop, Register data, Register value_klass) {
4675   // ((address) (void*) o) + vk->first_field_offset();
4676   Register offset = (data == oop) ? rscratch1 : data;
4677   first_field_offset(value_klass, offset);
4678   if (data == oop) {
4679     addptr(data, offset);
4680   } else {
4681     lea(data, Address(oop, offset));
4682   }
4683 }
4684 
4685 void MacroAssembler::data_for_value_array_index(Register array, Register array_klass,
4686                                                 Register index, Register data) {
4687   assert(index != rcx, "index needs to shift by rcx");
4688   assert_different_registers(array, array_klass, index);
4689   assert_different_registers(rcx, array, index);
4690 
4691   // array->base() + (index << Klass::layout_helper_log2_element_size(lh));
4692   movl(rcx, Address(array_klass, Klass::layout_helper_offset()));
4693 
4694   // Klass::layout_helper_log2_element_size(lh)
4695   // (lh >> _lh_log2_element_size_shift) & _lh_log2_element_size_mask;
4696   shrl(rcx, Klass::_lh_log2_element_size_shift);
4697   andl(rcx, Klass::_lh_log2_element_size_mask);
4698   shlptr(index); // index << rcx
4699 
4700   lea(data, Address(array, index, Address::times_1, arrayOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes(T_VALUETYPE)));
4701 }
4702 
4703 void MacroAssembler::resolve(DecoratorSet decorators, Register obj) {
4704   // Use stronger ACCESS_WRITE|ACCESS_READ by default.
4705   if ((decorators & (ACCESS_READ | ACCESS_WRITE)) == 0) {
4706     decorators |= ACCESS_READ | ACCESS_WRITE;
4707   }
4708   BarrierSetAssembler* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_assembler();
4709   return bs->resolve(this, decorators, obj);
4710 }
4711 
4712 void MacroAssembler::load_heap_oop(Register dst, Address src, Register tmp1,
4713                                    Register thread_tmp, DecoratorSet decorators) {
4714   access_load_at(T_OBJECT, IN_HEAP | decorators, dst, src, tmp1, thread_tmp);
4715 }
4716 
4717 // Doesn't do verfication, generates fixed size code
4718 void MacroAssembler::load_heap_oop_not_null(Register dst, Address src, Register tmp1,
4719                                             Register thread_tmp, DecoratorSet decorators) {
4720   access_load_at(T_OBJECT, IN_HEAP | IS_NOT_NULL | decorators, dst, src, tmp1, thread_tmp);
4721 }
4722 
4723 void MacroAssembler::store_heap_oop(Address dst, Register src, Register tmp1,
4724                                     Register tmp2, Register tmp3, DecoratorSet decorators) {
4725   access_store_at(T_OBJECT, IN_HEAP | decorators, dst, src, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3);
4726 }
4727 
4728 // Used for storing NULLs.
4729 void MacroAssembler::store_heap_oop_null(Address dst) {
4730   access_store_at(T_OBJECT, IN_HEAP, dst, noreg, noreg, noreg, noreg);
4731 }

4741 #ifdef ASSERT
4742 void MacroAssembler::verify_heapbase(const char* msg) {
4743   assert (UseCompressedOops, "should be compressed");
4744   assert (Universe::heap() != NULL, "java heap should be initialized");
4745   if (CheckCompressedOops) {
4746     Label ok;
4747     push(rscratch1); // cmpptr trashes rscratch1
4748     cmpptr(r12_heapbase, ExternalAddress((address)CompressedOops::ptrs_base_addr()));
4749     jcc(Assembler::equal, ok);
4750     STOP(msg);
4751     bind(ok);
4752     pop(rscratch1);
4753   }
4754 }
4755 #endif
4756 
4757 // Algorithm must match oop.inline.hpp encode_heap_oop.
4758 void MacroAssembler::encode_heap_oop(Register r) {
4759 #ifdef ASSERT
4760   verify_heapbase("MacroAssembler::encode_heap_oop: heap base corrupted?");
4761 #endif
4762   verify_oop_msg(r, "broken oop in encode_heap_oop");
4763   if (CompressedOops::base() == NULL) {
4764     if (CompressedOops::shift() != 0) {
4765       assert (LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes == CompressedOops::shift(), "decode alg wrong");
4766       shrq(r, LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes);
4767     }
4768     return;
4769   }
4770   testq(r, r);
4771   cmovq(Assembler::equal, r, r12_heapbase);
4772   subq(r, r12_heapbase);
4773   shrq(r, LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes);
4774 }
4775 
4776 void MacroAssembler::encode_heap_oop_not_null(Register r) {
4777 #ifdef ASSERT
4778   verify_heapbase("MacroAssembler::encode_heap_oop_not_null: heap base corrupted?");
4779   if (CheckCompressedOops) {
4780     Label ok;
4781     testq(r, r);
4782     jcc(Assembler::notEqual, ok);
4783     STOP("null oop passed to encode_heap_oop_not_null");
4784     bind(ok);
4785   }
4786 #endif
4787   verify_oop_msg(r, "broken oop in encode_heap_oop_not_null");
4788   if (CompressedOops::base() != NULL) {
4789     subq(r, r12_heapbase);
4790   }
4791   if (CompressedOops::shift() != 0) {
4792     assert (LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes == CompressedOops::shift(), "decode alg wrong");
4793     shrq(r, LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes);
4794   }
4795 }
4796 
4797 void MacroAssembler::encode_heap_oop_not_null(Register dst, Register src) {
4798 #ifdef ASSERT
4799   verify_heapbase("MacroAssembler::encode_heap_oop_not_null2: heap base corrupted?");
4800   if (CheckCompressedOops) {
4801     Label ok;
4802     testq(src, src);
4803     jcc(Assembler::notEqual, ok);
4804     STOP("null oop passed to encode_heap_oop_not_null2");
4805     bind(ok);
4806   }
4807 #endif
4808   verify_oop_msg(src, "broken oop in encode_heap_oop_not_null2");
4809   if (dst != src) {
4810     movq(dst, src);
4811   }
4812   if (CompressedOops::base() != NULL) {
4813     subq(dst, r12_heapbase);
4814   }
4815   if (CompressedOops::shift() != 0) {
4816     assert (LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes == CompressedOops::shift(), "decode alg wrong");
4817     shrq(dst, LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes);
4818   }
4819 }
4820 
4821 void  MacroAssembler::decode_heap_oop(Register r) {
4822 #ifdef ASSERT
4823   verify_heapbase("MacroAssembler::decode_heap_oop: heap base corrupted?");
4824 #endif
4825   if (CompressedOops::base() == NULL) {
4826     if (CompressedOops::shift() != 0) {
4827       assert (LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes == CompressedOops::shift(), "decode alg wrong");
4828       shlq(r, LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes);
4829     }
4830   } else {
4831     Label done;
4832     shlq(r, LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes);
4833     jccb(Assembler::equal, done);
4834     addq(r, r12_heapbase);
4835     bind(done);
4836   }
4837   verify_oop_msg(r, "broken oop in decode_heap_oop");
4838 }
4839 
4840 void  MacroAssembler::decode_heap_oop_not_null(Register r) {
4841   // Note: it will change flags
4842   assert (UseCompressedOops, "should only be used for compressed headers");
4843   assert (Universe::heap() != NULL, "java heap should be initialized");
4844   // Cannot assert, unverified entry point counts instructions (see .ad file)
4845   // vtableStubs also counts instructions in pd_code_size_limit.
4846   // Also do not verify_oop as this is called by verify_oop.
4847   if (CompressedOops::shift() != 0) {
4848     assert(LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes == CompressedOops::shift(), "decode alg wrong");
4849     shlq(r, LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes);
4850     if (CompressedOops::base() != NULL) {
4851       addq(r, r12_heapbase);
4852     }
4853   } else {
4854     assert (CompressedOops::base() == NULL, "sanity");
4855   }
4856 }
4857 
4858 void  MacroAssembler::decode_heap_oop_not_null(Register dst, Register src) {
4859   // Note: it will change flags
4860   assert (UseCompressedOops, "should only be used for compressed headers");
4861   assert (Universe::heap() != NULL, "java heap should be initialized");
4862   // Cannot assert, unverified entry point counts instructions (see .ad file)
4863   // vtableStubs also counts instructions in pd_code_size_limit.
4864   // Also do not verify_oop as this is called by verify_oop.
4865   if (CompressedOops::shift() != 0) {
4866     assert(LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes == CompressedOops::shift(), "decode alg wrong");
4867     if (LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes == Address::times_8) {
4868       leaq(dst, Address(r12_heapbase, src, Address::times_8, 0));
4869     } else {
4870       if (dst != src) {
4871         movq(dst, src);
4872       }
4873       shlq(dst, LogMinObjAlignmentInBytes);
4874       if (CompressedOops::base() != NULL) {
4875         addq(dst, r12_heapbase);
4876       }
4877     }
4878   } else {
4879     assert (CompressedOops::base() == NULL, "sanity");
4880     if (dst != src) {
4881       movq(dst, src);
4882     }
4883   }
4884 }
4885 
4886 void MacroAssembler::encode_klass_not_null(Register r) {
4887   if (CompressedKlassPointers::base() != NULL) {
4888     // Use r12 as a scratch register in which to temporarily load the narrow_klass_base.
4889     assert(r != r12_heapbase, "Encoding a klass in r12");
4890     mov64(r12_heapbase, (int64_t)CompressedKlassPointers::base());
4891     subq(r, r12_heapbase);
4892   }
4893   if (CompressedKlassPointers::shift() != 0) {
4894     assert (LogKlassAlignmentInBytes == CompressedKlassPointers::shift(), "decode alg wrong");
4895     shrq(r, LogKlassAlignmentInBytes);
4896   }
4897   if (CompressedKlassPointers::base() != NULL) {
4898     reinit_heapbase();
4899   }
4900 }
4901 
4902 void MacroAssembler::encode_klass_not_null(Register dst, Register src) {
4903   if (dst == src) {
4904     encode_klass_not_null(src);
4905   } else {
4906     if (CompressedKlassPointers::base() != NULL) {
4907       mov64(dst, (int64_t)CompressedKlassPointers::base());
4908       negq(dst);
4909       addq(dst, src);
4910     } else {
4911       movptr(dst, src);
4912     }
4913     if (CompressedKlassPointers::shift() != 0) {
4914       assert (LogKlassAlignmentInBytes == CompressedKlassPointers::shift(), "decode alg wrong");
4915       shrq(dst, LogKlassAlignmentInBytes);
4916     }
4917   }
4918 }
4919 
4920 // Function instr_size_for_decode_klass_not_null() counts the instructions
4921 // generated by decode_klass_not_null(register r) and reinit_heapbase(),
4922 // when (Universe::heap() != NULL).  Hence, if the instructions they
4923 // generate change, then this method needs to be updated.
4924 int MacroAssembler::instr_size_for_decode_klass_not_null() {
4925   assert (UseCompressedClassPointers, "only for compressed klass ptrs");
4926   if (CompressedKlassPointers::base() != NULL) {
4927     // mov64 + addq + shlq? + mov64  (for reinit_heapbase()).
4928     return (CompressedKlassPointers::shift() == 0 ? 20 : 24);
4929   } else {
4930     // longest load decode klass function, mov64, leaq
4931     return 16;
4932   }
4933 }
4934 
4935 // !!! If the instructions that get generated here change then function
4936 // instr_size_for_decode_klass_not_null() needs to get updated.
4937 void  MacroAssembler::decode_klass_not_null(Register r) {
4938   // Note: it will change flags
4939   assert (UseCompressedClassPointers, "should only be used for compressed headers");
4940   assert(r != r12_heapbase, "Decoding a klass in r12");
4941   // Cannot assert, unverified entry point counts instructions (see .ad file)
4942   // vtableStubs also counts instructions in pd_code_size_limit.
4943   // Also do not verify_oop as this is called by verify_oop.
4944   if (CompressedKlassPointers::shift() != 0) {
4945     assert(LogKlassAlignmentInBytes == CompressedKlassPointers::shift(), "decode alg wrong");
4946     shlq(r, LogKlassAlignmentInBytes);
4947   }
4948   // Use r12 as a scratch register in which to temporarily load the narrow_klass_base.
4949   if (CompressedKlassPointers::base() != NULL) {
4950     mov64(r12_heapbase, (int64_t)CompressedKlassPointers::base());
4951     addq(r, r12_heapbase);
4952     reinit_heapbase();
4953   }
4954 }
4955 
4956 void  MacroAssembler::decode_klass_not_null(Register dst, Register src) {
4957   // Note: it will change flags
4958   assert (UseCompressedClassPointers, "should only be used for compressed headers");
4959   if (dst == src) {
4960     decode_klass_not_null(dst);
4961   } else {
4962     // Cannot assert, unverified entry point counts instructions (see .ad file)
4963     // vtableStubs also counts instructions in pd_code_size_limit.
4964     // Also do not verify_oop as this is called by verify_oop.
4965     mov64(dst, (int64_t)CompressedKlassPointers::base());
4966     if (CompressedKlassPointers::shift() != 0) {
4967       assert(LogKlassAlignmentInBytes == CompressedKlassPointers::shift(), "decode alg wrong");
4968       assert(LogKlassAlignmentInBytes == Address::times_8, "klass not aligned on 64bits?");
4969       leaq(dst, Address(dst, src, Address::times_8, 0));
4970     } else {
4971       addq(dst, src);
4972     }
4973   }
4974 }
4975 
4976 void  MacroAssembler::set_narrow_oop(Register dst, jobject obj) {
4977   assert (UseCompressedOops, "should only be used for compressed headers");
4978   assert (Universe::heap() != NULL, "java heap should be initialized");
4979   assert (oop_recorder() != NULL, "this assembler needs an OopRecorder");
4980   int oop_index = oop_recorder()->find_index(obj);
4981   RelocationHolder rspec = oop_Relocation::spec(oop_index);
4982   mov_narrow_oop(dst, oop_index, rspec);
4983 }

4986   assert (UseCompressedOops, "should only be used for compressed headers");
4987   assert (Universe::heap() != NULL, "java heap should be initialized");
4988   assert (oop_recorder() != NULL, "this assembler needs an OopRecorder");
4989   int oop_index = oop_recorder()->find_index(obj);
4990   RelocationHolder rspec = oop_Relocation::spec(oop_index);
4991   mov_narrow_oop(dst, oop_index, rspec);
4992 }

5017 }

5019 void  MacroAssembler::cmp_narrow_oop(Address dst, jobject obj) {
5020   assert (UseCompressedOops, "should only be used for compressed headers");
5021   assert (Universe::heap() != NULL, "java heap should be initialized");
5022   assert (oop_recorder() != NULL, "this assembler needs an OopRecorder");
5023   int oop_index = oop_recorder()->find_index(obj);
5024   RelocationHolder rspec = oop_Relocation::spec(oop_index);
5025   Assembler::cmp_narrow_oop(dst, oop_index, rspec);
5026 }
5027 
5028 void  MacroAssembler::cmp_narrow_klass(Register dst, Klass* k) {
5029   assert (UseCompressedClassPointers, "should only be used for compressed headers");
5030   assert (oop_recorder() != NULL, "this assembler needs an OopRecorder");
5031   int klass_index = oop_recorder()->find_index(k);
5032   RelocationHolder rspec = metadata_Relocation::spec(klass_index);
5033   Assembler::cmp_narrow_oop(dst, CompressedKlassPointers::encode(k), rspec);
5034 }
5035 
5036 void  MacroAssembler::cmp_narrow_klass(Address dst, Klass* k) {
5037   assert (UseCompressedClassPointers, "should only be used for compressed headers");
5038   assert (oop_recorder() != NULL, "this assembler needs an OopRecorder");
5039   int klass_index = oop_recorder()->find_index(k);
5040   RelocationHolder rspec = metadata_Relocation::spec(klass_index);
5041   Assembler::cmp_narrow_oop(dst, CompressedKlassPointers::encode(k), rspec);
5042 }
5043 
5044 void MacroAssembler::reinit_heapbase() {
5045   if (UseCompressedOops || UseCompressedClassPointers) {
5046     if (Universe::heap() != NULL) {
5047       if (CompressedOops::base() == NULL) {
5048         MacroAssembler::xorptr(r12_heapbase, r12_heapbase);
5049       } else {
5050         mov64(r12_heapbase, (int64_t)CompressedOops::ptrs_base());
5051       }
5052     } else {
5053       movptr(r12_heapbase, ExternalAddress((address)CompressedOops::ptrs_base_addr()));
5054     }
5055   }
5056 }
5057 
5058 #endif // _LP64
5059 
5060 // C2 compiled method's prolog code.
5061 void MacroAssembler::verified_entry(Compile* C, int sp_inc) {
5062   int framesize = C->output()->frame_size_in_bytes();
5063   int bangsize = C->output()->bang_size_in_bytes();
5064   bool fp_mode_24b = false;
5065   int stack_bang_size = C->output()->need_stack_bang(bangsize) ? bangsize : 0;
5066 
5067   // WARNING: Initial instruction MUST be 5 bytes or longer so that
5068   // NativeJump::patch_verified_entry will be able to patch out the entry
5069   // code safely. The push to verify stack depth is ok at 5 bytes,
5070   // the frame allocation can be either 3 or 6 bytes. So if we don't do
5071   // stack bang then we must use the 6 byte frame allocation even if
5072   // we have no frame. :-(
5073   assert(stack_bang_size >= framesize || stack_bang_size <= 0, "stack bang size incorrect");
5074 
5075   assert((framesize & (StackAlignmentInBytes-1)) == 0, "frame size not aligned");
5076   // Remove word for return addr
5077   framesize -= wordSize;
5078   stack_bang_size -= wordSize;
5079 
5080   // Calls to C2R adapters often do not accept exceptional returns.
5081   // We require that their callers must bang for them.  But be careful, because
5082   // some VM calls (such as call site linkage) can use several kilobytes of
5083   // stack.  But the stack safety zone should account for that.
5084   // See bugs 4446381, 4468289, 4497237.
5085   if (stack_bang_size > 0) {
5086     generate_stack_overflow_check(stack_bang_size);
5087 
5088     // We always push rbp, so that on return to interpreter rbp, will be
5089     // restored correctly and we can correct the stack.
5090     push(rbp);
5091     // Save caller's stack pointer into RBP if the frame pointer is preserved.
5092     if (PreserveFramePointer) {
5093       mov(rbp, rsp);
5094     }
5095     // Remove word for ebp
5096     framesize -= wordSize;
5097 
5098     // Create frame
5099     if (framesize) {
5100       subptr(rsp, framesize);
5101     }
5102   } else {
5103     // Create frame (force generation of a 4 byte immediate value)
5104     subptr_imm32(rsp, framesize);
5105 
5106     // Save RBP register now.
5107     framesize -= wordSize;
5108     movptr(Address(rsp, framesize), rbp);
5109     // Save caller's stack pointer into RBP if the frame pointer is preserved.
5110     if (PreserveFramePointer) {
5111       movptr(rbp, rsp);
5112       if (framesize > 0) {
5113         addptr(rbp, framesize);
5114       }
5115     }
5116   }
5117 
5118   if (C->needs_stack_repair()) {
5119     // Save stack increment (also account for fixed framesize and rbp)
5120     assert((sp_inc & (StackAlignmentInBytes-1)) == 0, "stack increment not aligned");
5121     movptr(Address(rsp, C->output()->sp_inc_offset()), sp_inc + framesize + wordSize);
5122   }
5123 
5124   if (VerifyStackAtCalls) { // Majik cookie to verify stack depth
5125     framesize -= wordSize;
5126     movptr(Address(rsp, framesize), (int32_t)0xbadb100d);
5127   }
5128 
5129 #ifndef _LP64
5130   // If method sets FPU control word do it now
5131   if (fp_mode_24b) {
5132     fldcw(ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::addr_fpu_cntrl_wrd_24()));
5133   }
5134   if (UseSSE >= 2 && VerifyFPU) {
5135     verify_FPU(0, "FPU stack must be clean on entry");
5136   }
5137 #endif
5138 
5139 #ifdef ASSERT
5140   if (VerifyStackAtCalls) {
5141     Label L;
5142     push(rax);
5143     mov(rax, rsp);
5144     andptr(rax, StackAlignmentInBytes-1);
5145     cmpptr(rax, StackAlignmentInBytes-wordSize);
5146     pop(rax);
5147     jcc(Assembler::equal, L);
5148     STOP("Stack is not properly aligned!");
5149     bind(L);
5150   }
5151 #endif
5152 }
5153 
5154 // clear memory of size 'cnt' qwords, starting at 'base' using XMM/YMM registers
5155 void MacroAssembler::xmm_clear_mem(Register base, Register cnt, Register val, XMMRegister xtmp) {
5156   // cnt - number of qwords (8-byte words).
5157   // base - start address, qword aligned.
5158   Label L_zero_64_bytes, L_loop, L_sloop, L_tail, L_end;
5159   movdq(xtmp, val);
5160   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5161     punpcklqdq(xtmp, xtmp);
5162     vinserti128_high(xtmp, xtmp);
5163   } else {
5164     punpcklqdq(xtmp, xtmp);
5165   }
5166   jmp(L_zero_64_bytes);
5167 
5168   BIND(L_loop);
5169   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5170     vmovdqu(Address(base,  0), xtmp);
5171     vmovdqu(Address(base, 32), xtmp);
5172   } else {
5173     movdqu(Address(base,  0), xtmp);
5174     movdqu(Address(base, 16), xtmp);
5175     movdqu(Address(base, 32), xtmp);
5176     movdqu(Address(base, 48), xtmp);
5177   }
5178   addptr(base, 64);
5179 
5180   BIND(L_zero_64_bytes);
5181   subptr(cnt, 8);
5182   jccb(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_loop);
5183   addptr(cnt, 4);
5184   jccb(Assembler::less, L_tail);
5185   // Copy trailing 32 bytes
5186   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5187     vmovdqu(Address(base, 0), xtmp);
5188   } else {
5189     movdqu(Address(base,  0), xtmp);
5190     movdqu(Address(base, 16), xtmp);
5191   }
5192   addptr(base, 32);
5193   subptr(cnt, 4);
5194 
5195   BIND(L_tail);
5196   addptr(cnt, 4);
5197   jccb(Assembler::lessEqual, L_end);
5198   decrement(cnt);
5199 
5200   BIND(L_sloop);
5201   movq(Address(base, 0), xtmp);
5202   addptr(base, 8);
5203   decrement(cnt);
5204   jccb(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_sloop);
5205   BIND(L_end);
5206 }
5207 
5208 int MacroAssembler::store_value_type_fields_to_buf(ciValueKlass* vk, bool from_interpreter) {
5209   // A value type might be returned. If fields are in registers we
5210   // need to allocate a value type instance and initialize it with
5211   // the value of the fields.
5212   Label skip;
5213   // We only need a new buffered value if a new one is not returned
5214   testptr(rax, 1);
5215   jcc(Assembler::zero, skip);
5216   int call_offset = -1;
5217 
5218 #ifdef _LP64
5219   Label slow_case;
5220 
5221   // Try to allocate a new buffered value (from the heap)
5222   if (UseTLAB) {
5223     // FIXME -- for smaller code, the inline allocation (and the slow case) should be moved inside the pack handler.
5224     if (vk != NULL) {
5225       // Called from C1, where the return type is statically known.
5226       movptr(rbx, (intptr_t)vk->get_ValueKlass());
5227       jint lh = vk->layout_helper();
5228       assert(lh != Klass::_lh_neutral_value, "inline class in return type must have been resolved");
5229       movl(r14, lh);
5230     } else {
5231       // Call from interpreter. RAX contains ((the ValueKlass* of the return type) | 0x01)
5232       mov(rbx, rax);
5233       andptr(rbx, -2);
5234       movl(r14, Address(rbx, Klass::layout_helper_offset()));
5235     }
5236 
5237     movptr(r13, Address(r15_thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_top_offset())));
5238     lea(r14, Address(r13, r14, Address::times_1));
5239     cmpptr(r14, Address(r15_thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_end_offset())));
5240     jcc(Assembler::above, slow_case);
5241     movptr(Address(r15_thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_top_offset())), r14);
5242     movptr(Address(r13, oopDesc::mark_offset_in_bytes()), (intptr_t)markWord::always_locked_prototype().value());
5243 
5244     xorl(rax, rax); // use zero reg to clear memory (shorter code)
5245     store_klass_gap(r13, rax);  // zero klass gap for compressed oops
5246 
5247     if (vk == NULL) {
5248       // store_klass corrupts rbx, so save it in rax for later use (interpreter case only).
5249       mov(rax, rbx);
5250     }
5251     store_klass(r13, rbx);  // klass
5252 
5253     // We have our new buffered value, initialize its fields with a
5254     // value class specific handler
5255     if (vk != NULL) {
5256       // FIXME -- do the packing in-line to avoid the runtime call
5257       mov(rax, r13);
5258       call(RuntimeAddress(vk->pack_handler())); // no need for call info as this will not safepoint.
5259     } else {
5260       movptr(rbx, Address(rax, InstanceKlass::adr_valueklass_fixed_block_offset()));
5261       movptr(rbx, Address(rbx, ValueKlass::pack_handler_offset()));
5262       mov(rax, r13);
5263       call(rbx);
5264     }
5265     jmp(skip);
5266   }
5267 
5268   bind(slow_case);
5269   // We failed to allocate a new value, fall back to a runtime
5270   // call. Some oop field may be live in some registers but we can't
5271   // tell. That runtime call will take care of preserving them
5272   // across a GC if there's one.
5273 #endif
5274 
5275   if (from_interpreter) {
5276     super_call_VM_leaf(StubRoutines::store_value_type_fields_to_buf());
5277   } else {
5278     call(RuntimeAddress(StubRoutines::store_value_type_fields_to_buf()));
5279     call_offset = offset();
5280   }
5281 
5282   bind(skip);
5283   return call_offset;
5284 }
5285 
5286 
5287 // Move a value between registers/stack slots and update the reg_state
5288 bool MacroAssembler::move_helper(VMReg from, VMReg to, BasicType bt, RegState reg_state[], int ret_off, int extra_stack_offset) {
5289   if (reg_state[to->value()] == reg_written) {
5290     return true; // Already written
5291   }
5292   if (from != to && bt != T_VOID) {
5293     if (reg_state[to->value()] == reg_readonly) {
5294       return false; // Not yet writable
5295     }
5296     if (from->is_reg()) {
5297       if (to->is_reg()) {
5298         if (from->is_XMMRegister()) {
5299           if (bt == T_DOUBLE) {
5300             movdbl(to->as_XMMRegister(), from->as_XMMRegister());
5301           } else {
5302             assert(bt == T_FLOAT, "must be float");
5303             movflt(to->as_XMMRegister(), from->as_XMMRegister());
5304           }
5305         } else {
5306           movq(to->as_Register(), from->as_Register());
5307         }
5308       } else {
5309         int st_off = to->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset;
5310         assert(st_off != ret_off, "overwriting return address at %d", st_off);
5311         Address to_addr = Address(rsp, st_off);
5312         if (from->is_XMMRegister()) {
5313           if (bt == T_DOUBLE) {
5314             movdbl(to_addr, from->as_XMMRegister());
5315           } else {
5316             assert(bt == T_FLOAT, "must be float");
5317             movflt(to_addr, from->as_XMMRegister());
5318           }
5319         } else {
5320           movq(to_addr, from->as_Register());
5321         }
5322       }
5323     } else {
5324       Address from_addr = Address(rsp, from->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset);
5325       if (to->is_reg()) {
5326         if (to->is_XMMRegister()) {
5327           if (bt == T_DOUBLE) {
5328             movdbl(to->as_XMMRegister(), from_addr);
5329           } else {
5330             assert(bt == T_FLOAT, "must be float");
5331             movflt(to->as_XMMRegister(), from_addr);
5332           }
5333         } else {
5334           movq(to->as_Register(), from_addr);
5335         }
5336       } else {
5337         int st_off = to->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset;
5338         assert(st_off != ret_off, "overwriting return address at %d", st_off);
5339         movq(r13, from_addr);
5340         movq(Address(rsp, st_off), r13);
5341       }
5342     }
5343   }
5344   // Update register states
5345   reg_state[from->value()] = reg_writable;
5346   reg_state[to->value()] = reg_written;
5347   return true;
5348 }
5349 
5350 // Read all fields from a value type oop and store the values in registers/stack slots
5351 bool MacroAssembler::unpack_value_helper(const GrowableArray<SigEntry>* sig, int& sig_index, VMReg from, VMRegPair* regs_to,
5352                                          int& to_index, RegState reg_state[], int ret_off, int extra_stack_offset) {
5353   Register fromReg = from->is_reg() ? from->as_Register() : noreg;
5354   assert(sig->at(sig_index)._bt == T_VOID, "should be at end delimiter");
5355 
5356   int vt = 1;
5357   bool done = true;
5358   bool mark_done = true;
5359   do {
5360     sig_index--;
5361     BasicType bt = sig->at(sig_index)._bt;
5362     if (bt == T_VALUETYPE) {
5363       vt--;
5364     } else if (bt == T_VOID &&
